***uitgaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgaan.html>uitgaan</a> (3094)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ûtegâen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ūtgān</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgaan.html>uitgaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go out <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to go to public <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a> for leisure</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn off, to shut down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expire, to break up (of a relationship)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgang.html>uitgang</a> (3570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ūtgang</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ūtgang</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ūtgangaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ausgang</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">outgang</i>.
</p>

</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">electronics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> output</li>

***uitgave.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgave.html>uitgave</a> (12659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeven.html>uitgeven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to give out, to spend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgave.html>uitgave</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgave.html>uitgaves</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgaven.html>uitgaven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgave.html>uitgavetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">uitgaafje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>edition, e.g. of a publication</li>
<li>release, e.g. of an album</li>
<li>monetary expense</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">utegeven</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgever.html>uitgever</a> (5777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeven.html>uitgeven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to publish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgever.html>uitgever</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgevers.html>uitgevers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgever.html>uitgevertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>publisher</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgever.html>uitgever</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uithangen.html>uithangen</a> (6016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">utehangen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">uuthangen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">uythangen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uithangen.html>uithangen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>Jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You probably <a href = vnd.unilang:forgot.html>forgot</a> to <b>hang out</b> the laundry.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to act like, to behave like
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:clown.html>clown</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uithangen.html>uithangen</a></b></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">to <b>act like</b> a <a href = vnd.unilang:clown.html>clown</a></span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>Ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoon.html>gewoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> nazi <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uithangen.html>uithangen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ofzo.html>ofzo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duizenden.html>duizenden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doden.html>doden</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Are you now just going to <b>act like</b> a Nazi or what and kill thousands of people?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the sense "to act like", an accompanying noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> always preceded by the definite article, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> when the English equivalent would use an indefinite article. The accompanying noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually singular.
</p>
